The occasion was of Christmas celebration in Ryan International School, Shahjahanpur. The merriment started days before with varied activities where students expressed their excitement of the festival. And finally on 22 December the celebration took it height with a spe', ...', cial assembly organised by the ryanites at different levels. The assembly started seeking Lord Almighty\u2019s blessings saying the scripture reading, Lord\u2019s Prayer and special prayer followed by Praise & Worship songs giving glory to the Lord. The students of STD VIII and IX sang carols reflecting the joy. Later the students of STD IX & X presented the nativity scene. The School band also gave a melodious performance giving glory to the Lord Almighty. The celebration came to end by a \u2018Christmas message\u2019 delivered by the Principal on behalf of our mentors, our Respected Chairman Sir Dr. A.F Pinto and Esteemed Managing Director Madam Grace Pinto. The chief guest of the day Mr. Ram Ganesh \u2013D.M of Shahjahanpur and Mr.Deva ,bureau head of Dainik Jagran.. along with', ...',  the other dignitaries received the salute during the parade. The guests of honour present were Mr.K.N .Rai  G.M of DSCL Loni , Mrs .Mishra Social Worker , Mrs.Roopam Verma President of Roll ball Association and Mr.Amit Owner of dell computer world.',  The sports torch- symbol of harmony and goodwill  ,was carried by worthy sports persons Shibhu Pandit and Sanvi Verma. The chief guest received the torch and declared the sports meet open.',  During the oath taking ceremony Sports minister Mst . Rachit recited the pledge. ',  The Chief Guest  Mr.Ram Ganesh during his address stated that he was happy to be at the inaugural ceremony of Ryan Sports Meet -2016 . Sports is an important extracurricular activity, it releases mental tension, improves personality and develops public relationship. Everyday children should spare time for sports. He wished all the students good luck and thanked the management.',  Various sports events like  cycle race ,zig-zag race ,partner race, 100m race, 200m race, 400m race and 4X100m relay were witnessed. Winners were awarded with certificates and medals.',  The Principal  Ms.Varsha Agrawal in his address thanked convenors, staff of Ryan and all ryanites ,parent community and all present. ',  Principal  Ms.Varsha awarded the shield to the winning house team- Blue House and runners up team Red House. The occasion was of Christmas celebration in Ryan International School, Shahjahanpur. And finally on 22 December the celebration took it height with a spe', ...', cial assembly organised by the ryanites at different levels. The assembly started seeking Lord Almighty\u2019s blessings saying the scripture reading, Lord\u2019s Prayer and special prayer followed by Praise & Worship songs giving glory to the Lord. The chief guest of the day Mr. Ram Ganesh \u2013D.M of Shahjahanpur and Mr.Deva ,bureau head of Dainik Jagran.. along with', ...',  the other dignitaries received the salute during the parade. The guests of honour present were Mr.K.N .Rai  G.M of DSCL Loni , Mrs .Mishra Social Worker , Mrs.Roopam Verma President of Roll ball Association and Mr.Amit Owner of dell computer world.',  The sports torch- symbol of harmony and goodwill  ,was carried by worthy sports persons Shibhu Pandit and Sanvi Verma. The chief guest received the torch and declared the sports meet open.',  During the oath taking ceremony Sports minister Mst . Rachit recited the pledge. ',  The Chief Guest  Mr.Ram Ganesh during his address stated that he was happy to be at the inaugural ceremony of Ryan Sports Meet -2016 . Sports is an important extracurricular activity, it releases mental tension, improves personality and develops public relationship. Everyday children should spare time for sports. He wished all the students good luck and thanked the management.',  Various sports events like  cycle race ,zig-zag race ,partner race, 100m race, 200m race, 400m race and 4X100m relay were witnessed. Winners were awarded with certificates and medals.',  The Principal  Ms.Varsha Agrawal in his address thanked convenors, staff of Ryan and all ryanites ,parent community and all present. ',  Principal  Ms.Varsha awarded the shield to the winning house team- Blue House and runners up team Red House.
